(******************************************************************************************

 Evaluation of functions of partial setoids

 We defined the function space of partial setoids, and the next step is to define the
 evaluation morphism. Suppose that we have partial setoids `X` and `Y`. The evaluation
 morphism goes from the product of `X` and the exponential of `X` and `Y` to `Y`, so its
 underlying formula takes terms `x : X`, `f : exp_partial_setoid X Y`, and `y : Y`, and
 these terms satisfy the relation if `f` is defined and `(x , y) ∈ f`. In essence, this
 means that `x` is sent to `y` by `f`, and thus this formula describes evaluation.

 Content
 1. The formula of the evaluation morphism
 2. The laws of the evaluation morphism
 3. The evaluation morphism

 ******************************************************************************************)

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Hyperdoctrines.Tripos.

Local Open Scope cat.
Local Open Scope hd.

Section PEREvaluation.
  Context {H : tripos}
          (X Y : partial_setoid H).

  (** * 1. The formula of the evaluation morphism *)
  Definition eval_partial_setoid_form
    : form (prod_partial_setoid X (exp_partial_setoid X Y) ×h Y)
    := let x := π₁ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))) in
       let f := π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))) in
       let y := π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) in
       (exp_partial_setoid_is_function [ f ])
       ∧
       ⟨ x , y ⟩ ∈ f.

  Arguments eval_partial_setoid_form /.

  (** * 2. The laws of the evaluation morphism *)
  
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
partial_setoid_morphism_laws eval_partial_setoid_form

                    (π₁
                       (π₁
                          (π₁
                             (tm_var
                                ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (...))
                                   ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                  ×h Y) ×h Y))))) ~
                  π₂
                    (π₁
                       (π₁
                          (tm_var
                             ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                               ×h Y) ×h Y))))
                  ⇒ π₂
                      (π₁
                         (tm_var
                            ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                               ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                              ×h Y) ×h Y))) ~
                    π₂
                      (tm_var
                         ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                            ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)
                          ×h Y))
                    ⇒ (exp_partial_setoid_is_function
                       [π₂
                          (π₁
                             (tm_var
                                ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                 ×h Y)))]
                       ∧ ⟨ π₁
                             (π₁
                                (tm_var
                                   ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                    ×h Y))),
                         π₂
                           (tm_var
                              ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))
                         ⟩
                         ∈ π₂
                             (π₁
                                (tm_var
                                   ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                    ×h Y))))
                      [⟨ π₂
                           (π₁
                              (π₁
                                 (π₁
                                    (tm_var
                                       ((((𝟙 ×h ...)
                                          ×h X
                                             ×h ℙ ...)
                                         ×h Y) ×h Y))))),
                       π₂
                         (π₁
                            (tm_var
                               ((((𝟙
                                   ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                  ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                 ×h Y) ×h Y))) ⟩]
                      ⇒ (exp_partial_setoid_is_function
                         [π₂
                            (π₁
                               (tm_var
                                  ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                   ×h Y)))]
                         ∧ ⟨ π₁
                               (π₁
                                  (tm_var
                                     ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                      ×h Y))),
                           π₂
                             (tm_var
                                ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                 ×h Y)) ⟩
                           ∈ π₂
                               (π₁
                                  (tm_var
                                     ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                      ×h Y))))
                        [⟨ π₂
                             (π₁
                                (π₁
                                   (tm_var
                                      ((((𝟙
                                          ×h X
                                             ×h ℙ ...)
                                         ×h X
                                            ×h ℙ
                                                 (X
                                                 ×h Y))
                                        ×h Y) ×h Y)))),
                         π₂
                           (tm_var
                              ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                                ×h Y) ×h Y)) ⟩]))))

      
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
(((⊤ [π₁ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))])
  [π₁
     (tm_var
        ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))])
 [π₁
    (tm_var
       (((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
        ×h Y))])
[π₁
   (tm_var
      ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
        ×h Y) ×h Y))]
⊢ π₂
    (π₁
       (π₁
          (π₁
             (tm_var
                ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                   ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))))) ~
  π₂
    (π₁
       (π₁
          (tm_var
             ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))))
  ⇒ π₂
      (π₁
         (tm_var
            ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
               ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))) ~
    π₂
      (tm_var
         ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
           ×h Y) ×h Y))
    ⇒ (exp_partial_setoid_is_function
       [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))]
       ∧ ⟨ π₁ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))),
         π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩
         ∈ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))))
      [⟨ π₂
           (π₁
              (π₁
                 (π₁
                    (tm_var
                       ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                          ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)
                        ×h Y))))),
       π₂
         (π₁
            (tm_var
               ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                  ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))) ⟩]
      ⇒ (exp_partial_setoid_is_function
         [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))]
         ∧ ⟨ π₁ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))),
           π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩
           ∈ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))))
        [⟨ π₂
             (π₁
                (π₁
                   (tm_var
                      ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                         ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)
                       ×h Y)))),
         π₂
           (tm_var
              ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y)) ⟩]

      (π₁
         (tm_var
            ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
               ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))) ⟩
    ∈ π₂
        (π₂
           (π₁
              (π₁
                 (π₁
                    (tm_var
                       ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                          ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)
                        ×h Y))))))
⊢ exp_partial_setoid_is_function
  [π₂
     (π₂
        (π₁
           (π₁
              (tm_var
                 ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                    ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y)))))]
  ∧ ⟨ π₁
        (π₂
           (π₁
              (π₁
                 (tm_var
                    ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                       ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))))),
    π₂
      (tm_var
         ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
           ×h Y) ×h Y)) ⟩
    ∈ π₂
        (π₂
           (π₁
              (π₁
                 (tm_var
                    ((((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))
                       ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y)))))

        (tm_var

                     ((𝟙
                       ×h prod_partial_setoid X

             π₂
               (tm_var
                  ((𝟙
                    ×h prod_partial_setoid X
                         (exp_partial_setoid X Y))
                   ×h Y)) ⟩]))

   (tm_var
      (𝟙
       ×h prod_partial_setoid X
            (exp_partial_setoid X Y)))]
∧ π₂
    (tm_var
       (𝟙
        ×h prod_partial_setoid X
             (exp_partial_setoid X Y))) ~
  π₂
    (tm_var
       (𝟙
        ×h prod_partial_setoid X
             (exp_partial_setoid X Y)))
⊢ ∃h (eval_partial_setoid_form
      [⟨ (π₂
            (tm_var
               (𝟙
                ×h prod_partial_setoid X
                     (exp_partial_setoid X Y))))
         [π₁
            (tm_var
               ((𝟙
                 ×h prod_partial_setoid X
                      (exp_partial_setoid X Y)) ×h Y))
         ]tm,
       π₂
         (tm_var
            ((𝟙
              ×h prod_partial_setoid X
                   (exp_partial_setoid X Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩])

   [π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))))]
   ∧ exp_partial_setoid_eq
     [⟨ π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))),
      π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))) ⟩])
[π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))]
∧ ⟨ (π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))))
    [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ]tm,
  π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩
  ∈ (π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))))
    [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ]tm
⊢ (∃h ((exp_partial_setoid_is_function
        [π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))]
        ∧ ⟨ π₁ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))),
          π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩
          ∈ π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))))
       [⟨ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))))
          [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))
          ]tm,
        π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩]))
  [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))]

        
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
((π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))) ~
  π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))))
 [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))]
 ∧ exp_partial_setoid_is_function
   [(π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))))
    [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ]tm]
   ∧ exp_partial_setoid_eq
     [⟨ π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))),
      π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))) ⟩
      [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ]tm])
∧ ⟨ (π₁ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))))
    [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ]tm,
  π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩
  ∈ (π₂ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)))))
    [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ]tm
⊢ ∃h (exp_partial_setoid_is_function
      [(π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))))
       [⟨ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))))
          [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))
          ]tm,
        π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩
        [⟨ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))
           [π₁
              (tm_var
                 (((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))
           ]tm,
         π₂
           (tm_var
              (((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y)) ⟩
        ]tm ]tm]
      ∧ (tripos_in (X ×h Y))
        [⟨ ⟨ π₁ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))),
           π₂ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩,
         π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))) ⟩
         [⟨ (π₂ (tm_var (𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y))))
            [π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y))
            ]tm,
          π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)) ⟩
          [⟨ (π₁
                (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))
             [π₁
                (tm_var
                   (((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))
             ]tm,
           π₂
             (tm_var
                (((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) ×h Y))
           ⟩ ]tm ]tm])

X, Y: partial_setoid H
x:= π₁ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) X
f:= π₂ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) (ℙ (X ×h Y))
y:= π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) Y
(x ~ x
 ∧ exp_partial_setoid_is_function [f]
   ∧ exp_partial_setoid_eq [⟨ f, f ⟩]) ∧ ⟨ x, y ⟩ ∈ f
⊢ exp_partial_setoid_is_function [f]
H: tripos

x:= π₁ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) X
f:= π₂ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) (ℙ (X ×h Y))

H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
x:= π₁ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) X
f:= π₂ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) (ℙ (X ×h Y))
y:= π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) Y
exp_partial_setoid_is_function [f]
⊢ exp_partial_setoid_is_function [f]

             apply hyperdoctrine_hyp.
          
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
x:= π₁ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) X
f:= π₂ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) (ℙ (X ×h Y))
y:= π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) Y
(x ~ x
 ∧ exp_partial_setoid_is_function [f]
   ∧ exp_partial_setoid_eq [⟨ f, f ⟩]) ∧ ⟨ x, y ⟩ ∈ f
⊢ ⟨ x, y ⟩ ∈ f
 
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
x:= π₁ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) X
f:= π₂ (π₂ (π₁ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)))): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) (ℙ (X ×h Y))
y:= π₂ (tm_var ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y)): tm ((𝟙 ×h X ×h ℙ (X ×h Y)) ×h Y) Y
⟨ x, y ⟩ ∈ f ⊢ ⟨ x, y ⟩ ∈ f

             apply hyperdoctrine_hyp.
  Qed.

  (** * 3. The evaluation morphism *)
  
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
partial_setoid_morphism
  (prod_partial_setoid X (exp_partial_setoid X Y)) Y

  
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
partial_setoid_morphism
  (prod_partial_setoid X (exp_partial_setoid X Y)) Y

    
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
form
  (prod_partial_setoid X (exp_partial_setoid X Y) ×h Y)
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
partial_setoid_morphism_laws ?φ

    
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
form
  (prod_partial_setoid X (exp_partial_setoid X Y) ×h Y)
 exact eval_partial_setoid_form.
    
H: tripos
X, Y: partial_setoid H
partial_setoid_morphism_laws eval_partial_setoid_form
 exact eval_partial_setoid_laws.
  Defined.
End PEREvaluation.
